--
-- Table structure for table `cargos_competencias`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `cargos_competencias`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `cargos_competencias` (
  `id_relacion` int(6) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `comp_g_id_comp` int(2) NOT NULL,
  `cargos_id_cargo` int(6) NOT NULL,
  `grado` int(2) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id_relacion`),
  KEY `id_cargos` (`comp_g_id_comp`,`cargos_id_cargo`),
  KEY `cargos_id_cargo` (`cargos_id_cargo`),
  CONSTRAINT `cargos_competencias_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`comp_g_id_comp`) REFERENCES `competencias` (`id_competencia`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `cargos_competencias_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`cargos_id_cargo`) REFERENCES `cargos` (`id_cargo`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1525 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;
